<b>Stéphane Humbert Lucas 777</b> is a Oriental Woody fragrance for women and men. <b>Mortal Skin</b> was launched in 2015. The nose behind this fragrance is Stephane Humbert Lucas. Top notes are Ink, Blackberry, Incense and Labdanum; middle notes are Myrrh, Opoponax, Iris, Cardamom and Artemisia; base notes are Styrax, Ambergris, Atlas Cedar, Cedar, Sandalwood, Birch and Musk. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>Niche perfumer Stéphane Humbert Lucas launches his new fragrance Mortal Skin in 2015, the first fragrance of The Snake Collection, unlike the rest which belong to the 777 collection. The fragrance is smoky, oriental - woody. </p>

<p>
“1st Act: The perfume, languid and colourful, hypnotises me,
I am facing two eyes that desire me.
Leafy coolness, fruits, the magic of the encounter,
The seduction begins.</p>

<p>2nd Act:
The perfume rises up and paralyses me,
The fangs ooze, wanting to sink into me.
Throbbing heat mixed with blue cold, I think I am bitten.
Sandalwood, tequila, intoxication.</p>

<p>3rd Act:
Bestiality, brutality, journey,
The perfume smells of hot ash.
Life slips away.
It now knows that all is beautiful.</p>

<p> Top notes: blackberry, ink, incense and labdanum. Heart: opoponax, iris, davana, myrrh and cardamom. Base: ambergris, styrax, sandalwood, labdanum, civet, cedar, birch and musk. </p>

How much does this cost!?? But it really is a second skin scent and as I became familiar with it the nuance of the inky blackberry, sweet resins, faint incense iris, and wood it opened up to me. It’s distinct but not obvious you are wearing a fragrance. <br />
<br />
My wife smelled my wrist and remarked that it reminded her of clean diapers, pleasant but not the association you might want with a scent. It does smell like clean skin so maybe that’s it. Won’t be for everyone but this made me warm up to the idea of skin scents in general. align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="2237136"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=2237136#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2230649" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2230649" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Scratch &amp; Sniff"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1878218"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1878218.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Scratch &amp; Sniff" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2230649ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2230649" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1878218">Scratch &amp; Sniff</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-26">07/26/24 23:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Zoologist Black Mamba, is that you?<br />
<br />
Inspired by the viper snake, this scent could very well be a part of the Zoologist perfume line (which is a compliment and a full-bellied glowing endorsement).  In fact, with its primary ink note, Mortal Skin is highly reminiscent of Zoologist’s Squid: these two could be sister scents.  Except, whereas Squid is a marine scent from the oceanic depths, Mortal Skin is more woodsy and  fruity with its blackberry note, which stops just short of entering gourmand terrain.  Similar to Squid, the ink is front and center here, and it spills across your mortal skin like a heavy, wet, delicious, black stain.  Yet, Mortal Skin proves to be an entirely different animal from Squid, given the additional notes of blackberry, resin, and the faintest hint of iris.<br />
<br />
Ink, fruit, and woods: Mortal Skin is an enigma and challenging to describe.  But let me tell you this…<br />
<br />
This scent still fucks.  It’s art, and it's the definition of niche perfumery.  It’s sex in a bottle.  It’s masculine and sleek, like a serpent’s scales.  It’s like being thrown into the Indiana Jones snake pit - except that pit is a black pool of watery ink with black mambas and blackberries skimming and floating on the surface like black rose petals.  The only problem is that pool goes dry quickly, as the longevity on this is quite weak.<br />
<br />
But above all else, Mortal Skin is tempting.  It’s the snake in the Garden of Eden, flicking its tongue against your ear and daring you not to eat the apple, but rather the blackberry.  "The darker the berry, the sweeter the juice," the snake hisses.  As you give in and spray this, biting into that poisoned berry, you can feel the sweet black juice oozing and dribbling down your neck and wrists, as your eyes turn pitch-black and vampiric.  Then the snake wraps its coils around you further, and it tempts you to pull out your credit card to drop $230.00 on this bottle of precious venom.<br />
<br />
Go on, give into your basic instincts and buy the bottle.  Both sin and skin never smelled so good.<br />
<br />
In five words or less: Squid, but make it viper.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="2230649"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=2230649#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2213036" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Very seductive, not too dark and will generally be more mass-appealing than other fragrances with similar scent accords.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="2153694"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=2153694#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2130359" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Has good sillage and longevity, but the ink/resins ended up being too much for me. I really like the iris and blackberry notes in this though.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="2110220"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=2110220#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2097063" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2097063" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="RGH01"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1331188"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1331188.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="RGH01" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2097063ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2097063" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1331188">RGH01</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-19">03/19/24 03:37</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Mortal Skin is one of the more unique creations from Stephane Humbert Lucas, tying in an array of strange and unusual notes and yet has housed them together beautifully. All in all this is a resinous incense-based fragrance; the thick, chewy nature of myrrh, opoponax and styrax mingle to create that incredibly dark yet alluring smoky feel.<br />
<br />
Alongside this is the dominant note of blackberry, with its sweet juiciness subdued by a heavy dose of thick black ink. This juxtaposes the delicious aura of the blackberry with something far more bitter and brooding. A leathery labdanum and smooth woody base finish this scent of to perfection.<br />
<br />
This scent is a fantastically though-provoking creation, definitely a fragrance to stand out from the crowd. I’m not sure it’s exactly my style but I can appreciate the creativity and passion that’s gone into making this.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="2097063"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=2097063#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2075904" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2056611" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="brumbarche"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1001822"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1001822.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="brumbarche" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2056611ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2056611" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1001822">brumbarche</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-08">02/08/24 17:37</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Smooth and quiet. Gloomy, but interesting. Mysterious, like smoky eyes. Polarizing too, imo. I like it a lot. Not for the price, though. Billie Eilish 2 is in the same alley and this is the price I’d expect for a scent with such profile.<br />
<br />
I often layer Jo Malone Blackberry &amp; Bay with Miller Harris Tender in order to achieve this deep dark pastel grey color that I crave at times.<br />
It’s not the same ofc. MS in comparison feels more gloomy, but peppery warm; of sweeter and more dense resins (the oppoponax) and it’s more inky. There’s something about it that feels cozy but ozonic, like the air in a warm damp secluded basement with a private swimming pool in it (chlorinated water vapor). <br />
While the combo I use is watercolor, more powdery, floral, pepper-minty (the bayleaf) and lacks the resinous touch (which perfumes like Memo Shams Oud , ADO Larmes du Desert, Smoking Hot etc .. have, without the ink that’s here), more airy. <br />
I’m mentioning all this so that you can see how it’s not easy to get a good idea of what the perfume is like from a mere description, or praise or negative comments. So, no matter who says what about how good it is - one thing is for sure - this is not a safe blindbuy. It needs extensive testing. It is unusual. It gives me this funeral home vibe. I like it, but in a twisted way. I think it’s not something most people would wear to appeal to others, but I can see how it can work well if you are a mortician or attending a funeral or nail it on Halloween dressed as a sophisticated, but somehow sensual pale vampire hosting a basement pool party.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Its shedding of skin represents spiritual awakening and for some cultures the life cycle of death and rebirth.<br />
Mortal Skin is enveloping and mysterious, captivating with notes of ink and blackberry and then with a dusty Iris, which I perceive a lot on my skin.<br />
The resins and woods enrich it but in my opinion it is such a successful alchemy that it is very difficult to speak about single notes.<br />
It's intriguing, sinuous and I really like it.<br />
A great mess about the performance, which is average, I would have preferred it to last longer.<br />

<br />

<br />
This bottle is so freaking cool too. My new favorite bottle in my collection (sorry, Electimuss)<br />
<br />

<br />

<br />
Scent - 9/10<br />
Bottle - 10/10<br />
Longevity - 8.5/10<br />
Projection - 6/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="1952163"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=1952163#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1918366" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1345688">RhettB27</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-06-05">06/05/23 19:40</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It’s taken some time to fully appreciate Mortal Skin. I got my bottle 4-5 months ago and I initially wasn’t too keen on it. It’s unapologetic at first but it dries into a gorgeous rich, smoky, and ambery incense that becomes an experience rather than just a fragrance. It possesses a smokey leathery facet from the labdanum, birch, and styrax most likely, with spicy warm balsamic qualities from the myrrh/sweet myrrh working with it. It’s mysterious and refined, on the darker side, but it wears surprisingly easy especially after an hour or so. Great performance and it leans masculine to me, but part of the beauty of fragrances is how they personally morph with you. I’d say Mortal Skin is a top tier incense fragrance that offers unique qualities and ultimately doesn’t wear as heavy as you would initially expect it to.<br />
Btw I layered Initio Blessed Baraka under this to sweeten it up some and damn…just amazing 🤤</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="1849945"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=1849945#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1849598" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; There’s also a little leathery vibe going on that is not off-putting and works well with all that’s going on. It does ultimately dry down into a soft Iris sandalwood that has a little warmth, maybe 3-5 hours in. It’s never that loud to begin with but it softens even more and again sums up to be a nice powdery woody scent in the end. Very pleasant, kind of hard to hate which is quite funny given the notes listed.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="1678813"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=1678813#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1658778" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1263755">The Wolf</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-10-04">10/04/22 09:18</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Once in a blue moon I come across something so unique that it's difficult to describe and put in a bucket with similar fragrances. Mortal Skin does not smell like anything I've tried, so there's no point of reference but I'll try. Opening and middle I get mainly blackberry, ink, and incense. It smells very cold, very complex, and mysterious. Beyond that, musk, orris, and unique suede comes out.<br />
<br />
A friend described this to me as how he would imagine a snakes skin to smell and I agree. It does have a snake/alligator skin vibe. If I had to compare, it reminds me a little bit of Etat Libre D'Orange Rien, little bit of Tom Ford Fabulous, and Jubilation XXV mixed together. Very interesting option for the cold weather. This is art, but also wearable art that smells good! There's something addictive about this one one. Absolutely bottle worthy.. <br />
<br />
Scent 9.5/10<br />
Performance 7/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="1658778"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=1658778#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1657392" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I notice a lot of resins and a slightly salty ambergris note. The artemsia adds a very subtle greenness, and i pick up some dusty iris and sour cardamom.<br />
<br />
The scent is pretty toned down though, it doesn't jump off the strip at me at all.<br />
<br />
There's not a ton of sweetness here, but nothing that makes the scent too masculine either. This is unisex enough that a woman can wear it without feeling like they're using their husband's cologne.<br />
<br />
I don't dislike this offering but it's not especially mind-blowing for me either. If you want a kind of gothic, dark mysterious scent that doesn't have too overwhelming of a presence (and doesn't contain any rose, saffron or patchouli notes), i think this is a good choice.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1255031" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="kateapple"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/440921"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.440921.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="kateapple" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-Eau-de-Parfum-52359.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.52359.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Chance Eau Tendre Eau de Parfum"title="Chance Eau Tendre Eau de Parfum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1255031ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1255031" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.84); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/440921">kateapple</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-11-30">11/30/20 19:57</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A dichotomy of warm and chilly. <br />
<br />
I was actually quite nervous to try this one. The reviews were crazy, the ink note was strange, and of course the bottle looks intimidating. However, it was much more subdued than I imagined. After smelling ink in another scent and disliking it, this one put some fear into me, but I was just too curious to resist.<br />
<br />
This scent combines what I can only describe as a chilled blackberry with a warm myrrh. The blackberry almost feels like it's mixed with mint, but I think it's actually the ink note that's giving it an odd chill. Pair this with a gorgeous, resinous cloud of myrrh and the scent is unique for sure, but not necessarily unusual.<br />
<br />
I don't find that this feel venemous or intimidating at all. I'm quite surprised at how well the blackberry/"ink" combo mixes with the myrrh...it doesn't feel too disjointed. You can still pick them out as two distinct vibes, though.<br />
<br />
Like all other reviews of this, I don't think I can do this justice. It's not a matter of whether or not this is good, it's just a bit indescribable...but in a subtle way. I was not bombarded with a bizarre ink note, overly-sour berries, or sickly sweet resins. It's all quite subdued and intriguing.<br />
<br />
If your interest has been piqued, try it. No review can convey exactly what this is like. I don't say this to hype it up as some ingenious work or masterpiece, it's just unlike any combination of notes I've smelled before, and I'm surprised that it works so well. It's worth trying at least once, just to see.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="1255031"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=1255031#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1236959" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1206888" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="17seyed"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1165604"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1165604.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="17seyed" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1206888ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1206888" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1165604">17seyed</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-08-02">08/02/20 23:40</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>W̶h̶o̶ What are you?<br />
<br />
If Stephane Humbert Lucas told me that there's a real snake hidden inside Mortal Skin, I would believe him. The fragrance seems to shed skin and present a different side of itself each time I wear it.<br />
<br />
Sometimes it opens with a beautifully dark and cold blackberry that is spiced up by cardamom, and dries down a wonderful buttery iris laying on a bed of myrrh and almond. This variation reminds me a little bit of Bois d'Argent and Rolling in Love.<br />
<br />
And sometimes, it has a venomous and photorealistic opening of ink that is made even more bitter with artemisia, and dries down to a robust concoction of resinous opoponax with an animallic touch of a combination between musk and ambergris. This variation reminds me a little bit of Tobacco Oud.<br />
<br />
A dark shadow of incense looms over the composition regardless of which variation decides to show itself that day.<br />
<br />
Mortal Skin is what I consider to be my favorite type of estoric niche perfumery, where the artist creates a unique and engaging fragrance that will not only intrigue your olfactory senses, but also pleases them. That's what I love about Mortal Skin; is that all artistic merit aside, it smells GOOD. Unlike many other "niche" fragrances that think they are the pinnacle of innovation just because they reek of fecal oud and other novelty notes.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="1206888"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=1206888#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1197543" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1197543" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="C-Sauce"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1090845"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1090845.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="C-Sauce" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1197543ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1197543" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1090845">C-Sauce</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-07-08">07/08/20 21:08</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I love this scent. It is perfect for a cool, quiet summer night. It is introspective, reclusive, silent.<br />
<br />
It is “Mortal Skin,” after all, hence it is no surprise that it sits close to the skin. In this way, it is reminiscent of Hamlet’s line, “when we have shuffled off this mortal coil.” The scent’s composition suits the mood and subject of that soliloquy: “To be or not to be, that is the question.” The scent’s performance presents the same dilemma. It slips in and out of perception like a snake in the grass.<br />
<br />
In moderate weather, the longevity is about 6-10 hours. It lasts on clothing for about 12 hours. The sillage is soft. Put it in an atomizer and bring it with you because the top notes are exquisite.<br />
<br />
Cool blackberry mist over almond powder.<br />
<br />
Scent: 10/10<br />
Sillage: soft (Up to 4 feet / light texture)<br />
Longevity: 6-12 hours<br />
Versatility: mainly quiet nights and close encounters</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="1197543"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=1197543#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1196819" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1196494">nightcrawler12101995</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-07-06">07/06/20 22:41</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>9/10- The scent of Maleficent.<br />
<br />
Scent nature is Dark Fruity Balsamic (Clubbing category).<br />
I'd use the words Alluring, Mysterious, and Poison to describe this scent.<br />
<br />
100%, Maleficent would wear this, I'd actually expect this juice to be bottled within Dior's Poison.<br />
<br />
Opoponax and Blackberry give the seductive sweetness which I find to be more mysterious than the Raspberry sweetness in Tuscan leather.<br />
<br />
Mortal Skin might smell juvenile for men over 40 while still being suitable for women of all ages.<br />
<br />
Note: The Inky note is quite discrete from the inkiness in Encre Noire, and the fragrance is not smoky but incensy which is more like an incense accord you smell from an ambient candle than burning actual incense.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1141379">AndySmellsGreat</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-06-28">06/28/20 18:44</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Another amazing 777 concoction...<br />
<br />
One of my favourite left field scents.<br />
<br />
Sweet not too pungent ink/blood with a sweet damp grass...<br />
<br />
I can imagine (actually have experienced) a snake living in a glass tank soiled with urine dead insects, damp humid greenery and dead tree limbs and the sickly sweet anamalic scent eminating creating an impression of an earthy den and a snake waiting to strike!<br />
<br />
That’s what it represents when you know the packaging and the story.<br />
<br />
When you don’t it comes across as a gorgeous somewhat dark sweet resinous syrupy ink with dark berry - slightly vanillic even (despite notes). Mysterious, animalac, dark and brooding on a male (something a well dressed gentlemanly vigorous vampire would wear). On a woman - gourmand, sultry, elegant - she’d be wearing a figure hugging dress and sensual and then like a Preying Mantis would sink her teeth into you during copulation. Think Eva Green in Dark Shadows.<br />
<br />
Not for whimps - which is why Escoteric I guess has a problem with it. It’s borderline left field - phenomenal performance and a great bubble - the bottle design is also a statement deserving a place on your mantle as well. Don’t over analyse this though - for some this is will be just a gorgeous dark sweet gourmand.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="1193906"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=1193906#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1187224" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; This is a nice office fragrance. It comes across slightly effeminate early to mid, amber vanilla becoming increasingly peppery with sandalwood and settling close to the skin. That's it.<br />
Now , of course, if you look at the notes, you start thinking, wow! Of course! I can smell blackberry, iris, Myrrh, musk, how clever, I can really appreciate this.<br />
However in the real world that is not what you will be thinking. In fact instead you will be crying with the knowledge you could smell a lot better for a lot less.<br />
This is one for the Tate Gallery for the cognoscenti to admire in their own time at their own expense.<br />
I have Nasomatto's Absinth on my other arm. Now you're talking! Expensive but unique great sillage and longevity and gives simple souls  like me pleasure.<br />
<br />
Fragrance: 4/10 considering the expense. Otherwise 6.5/10 at face value.<br />
Projection: 6/10<br />
Longevity: 8/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="1130791"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=1130791#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1061996" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1043245" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="landshark321"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/888664"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.888664.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="landshark321" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1043245ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1043245" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/888664">landshark321</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-03-21">03/21/19 09:01</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>My first try from Stephane Humbert Lucas, but perhaps the house's best-known entry, Mortal Skin, is primarily a resinous fragrance, but with some interesting quirks.<br />
<br />
Admittedly I didn’t think it would smell like skin, but through the semi-animalic resinous dominance of the fragrance, it does vaguely have that vibe.  Some florals, the musk, and sandalwood bring the resins to a more comforting, semi-feminine place but there are other elements that frankly complicate the mix like blackberry, ink, and civet.  So its center is the resin/wood/musk dynamic but it does veer off interestingly with almost a powdery lipstick mix, so it seems a little feminine on my skin, but I like it.<br />
<br />
It’s not a huge performer, though, at least on me, and so at its pricing of $290 for 50ml is a bit steep as far as a full bottle.  I’ll enjoy trying this some more but with resinous fragrance—though I love them—I can be pretty picky, and Mortal Skin in particular is a “like” not a “love” for me, at least for now.<br />
<br />
7 out of 10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="1043245"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=1043245#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1011970" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Meztelenül állunk egy kristálytiszta térben, az abszolút sötétségben, bőrünkön érezzük a világegyetem, az örök éjszaka lüktetését, a távolban égő haldokló csillagködök lassú hullámzását, melyek csak az ionizált anyaguk miatt világítanak. A halandó bőr és egy összeomló távoli csillag feszültséggel teli illata…<br />
Az utazás mesésen indul, fekete tinta füstös tömjénnel párosul, egyesülésüket a kardamom is támogatja, mindehhez a gyanták kellő meleget kölcsönöznek az írisz fagyosságával szemben. Finom füst lebeg mindenfelé, olyan érzésünk támad, hogy mindez az élet törékenységéről szól, melyet körülvesz a nyírfából, szantálfából és cédrusból készült erős keret. <br />
Mindehhez nagy koncentrációban csatlakozik a parfüm tökéletes egyediségét biztosító, pézsmába és forró tintába mártott szeder igen különös illata. A háttérben egy száraz, illuzórikus zúgó erdőt hallunk, amely tényleg csak egy káprázat, hiszen valójában az erdő egy sima üvegre festett kép csupán. <br />
Ez nem az a fajta parfüm, amelyet egyszerűen csak viselünk, ez olyan, amit akkor kívánunk meg, amikor olyan emberrel találkozunk, akivel érdemes együtt lenni, és amikor felnézünk az égre, tudjuk, hogy nem vagyunk egyedül.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1065148">trabuquera</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2018-08-12">08/12/18 11:26</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This one makes me melancholy, because I keep sensing that there are wonderful things in there about to do something spectacular, but these fireworks lurk eternally out of reach ... there's something evanescent and elusive about every note, so I can't settle in and enjoy it. Could be an individual chemistry thing, but MY mortal skin seemed to first mute this down to a gently spiced powdery-wood with a few almost imperceptible sparks of iris ... didn't get the burst of blackberry or ink or darkness I was primed to expect ... and then I'd get the occasional waft of something wonderful every 10 minutes or so, but on burying my nose back to my wrist, it just wasn't there. Any trace of its loveliness entirely gone in 4h or so. So... not sure if I'm anosmic to it, or if it just doesn't perform on me, but this one was definitively NOT as billed. From the pyramid here I hoped for something rich, dark, almost boozily intoxicating, whereas Mortal Skin turned out to be a very subtle, adult, discreet performer. I worried I'd fall expensively in love with this one, but although I'm really glad to have tried it, am relieved to find that it's not meant to be. Unarguably a class act and a beautiful, complex scent if it works for you, though.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="971120"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=971120#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent934464" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="918544"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=918544#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent908405" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc908405" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="StellaDiverFlynn"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/475352"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.475352.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="StellaDiverFlynn" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Dame-Perfumery/Chocolate-Perfume-Oil-43159.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.43159.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Chocolate Perfume Oil"title="Chocolate Perfume Oil"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma908405ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd908405" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/475352">StellaDiverFlynn</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2018-02-05">02/05/18 14:08</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Mortal Skin is quite an abstract perfume on my skin. The notes blend and percolate through each other, that the smell as a whole, feels like an object exhibiting inflections of different notes. The evolution also takes place in a incremental manner, although three different phases can be distinguished on my skin.<br />
<br />
The first 30 minutes of Mortal Skin is a chewy, almost chalk-like musk to my nose, with abstract berry sweetness and clean "ozonic" feeling lifting the fragrance up without actually smelling like marine or ozonic elements, which is probably the "ink" referred to in the note list. <br />
<br />
The woody elements then become stronger with time, as well as the berry sweetness turns more sugary in parallel. There is also an almost oily creamy resin undertone and a saffron-like bitter fruitiness.  The combined effect of musky, resinous and slightly inky wood and sweet berries, actually strongly reminds me of the synthetic oud dry down in certain western brands. <br />
<br />
Like many western "oud" fragrances, Mortal Skin turns drier towards the dry down, but thankfully not as harsh as a few overdosed by woody amber aromachemicals. A simultaneously balmy, date-like and cool, mineral myrrh also comes to rescue, which makes a sweet balsamic berry skin scent with an interesting bitter twang.<br />
<br />
Mortal Skin stays mostly close to skin and lasts about at least 9 hours.<br />
<br />
I find it interesting that Mortal Skin is not as heavy as the note list suggests, which allows me to enjoy the fragrance even though I'm not so keen on occidental "oud" and sweet berry in general. But it also leaves me somewhat underwhelmed by this overall nebulous trail, especially at this price. If you happen to be looking for a soft, sweet "oud" and myrrh fragrance and has less limit on budget, Mortal Skin might be a contender, but I would otherwise hesitate to recommend it due to its price and accessibility.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="908405"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=908405#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent903435" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It's really familiar and different at the same time as another reviewer mentioned. It reminds me of d&amp;g the one and Mugler pure wood but doesn't really smell like either. To me it is a bit linear, starting off just a bit moist and finishing off just a bit dry. I don't get blackberry or ink (not that I really know what ink is supposed to smell like) but I do get something milky and powdery and dark. This part reminds me of Odin #10 but without the coconut. Literal and primary definition of "bestiality":<br />
<br />
"savagely cruel or depraved behaviour"<br />
<br />
The secondary meaning is sexual intercourse between human and animal. <br />
<br />
Given the context in which the word has been used, the editor/copy writer for the perfume clearly intends its use to infer the primary - not secondary - definition.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; It begins with a note of ink, leather and blackberry which dries down to reveal notes of styrax, opoponax, cardamom, iris, sandalwood, myrrh, cedar, birch, ambergris, and civet. This unisex perfume with moderate to strong sillage and longevity needs an adventurous and open mind to appreciate the interplay of dark animalic and somewhat lighter woody light spice notes. The feeling created is right on - a mysterious, slithery, viper nestled among the forest vines. Enjoy!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="853507"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=853507#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent825751" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc825751" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="SuzanneS"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/989138"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.989138.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="SuzanneS" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Ulric-de-Varens/Gold-Issime-10421.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.10421.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Gold Issime"title="Gold Issime"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma825751ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd825751" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/989138">SuzanneS</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2017-05-24">05/24/17 19:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Mortal Skin.<br />
<br />
Stephane Humbert Lucas can be counted on to provide intrigue, masterful blending and a story. <br />
<br />
I love this opening of sweet blackberry ink and rock rose reminiscent of the amber used in O'Hira. The incense and myrrh swirl around to add interest yet something is familiar. The polished cold-sweet iris rises in the heart much like Iris Fauve by Atelier des Ors. <br />
<br />
The slight forest like apparition reminds me of Galaad by Lubin when it is in its woody myrrh notes. There is a leathery nuance, and ambergris marine note as well keeping this dark, cool, smooth, animalic and supple.<br />
<br />
The notes could suggest a heavy beast however the delivery is light, lithe and clean. I suppose its because the synthetics are wielded very adeptly in this story. Out of all the fragrances mentioned..Mortal Skin rises above them all for me in terms of wear ability. Silage is light to moderate, an exemplary fruity iris woody oriental. Longevity is excellent. Sexy Intrigue in a bottle. If you want something unique, artistic and wearable.. Mortal Skin.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="825751"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=825751#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent807545" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/516615">SumoTigerCat</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2017-03-07">03/07/17 15:27</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>My husband writes calligraphy at times, and he always uses a fountain pen for general writing.  One of the inks that he uses is a brand “Iroshizuku”.  The colors are rich; the ink is smooth.  The bottles are simple and elegantly beautiful.  When I wear Mortal Skin, I think of the darkest colors of this ink.<br />
<br />
A kind member sent me a sample of Mortal Skin quite some time ago.  I was smitten, but the price at that time was something that I’d only spend on a rare Guerlain… maybe.  So, for many months, I kept stalking online sites with a wild hope of finding one I might afford.  As good fortune would have it, another member with whom I’ve traded several times had an almost full, with total presentation bottle for trade.  I hemmed and hawed, and cursed.  She kindly accepted my trade offer of a very HTF bottle.  I sighed a bit, and then danced for joy!<br />
<br />
Mortal Skin is not similar to the other Stéphane Humbert Lucas fragrances that I’ve tried. In my opinion, this is the nicest one.  Unique in its’ stark beauty.  I adore the ink note that underlies the scent throughout its’ wearing.  If there were such a thing as Blackberry Ink, this would be it.  The other notes that talk to me are the myrrh, incense, artemisia (yes, a faint whiff of absinthe), and cardamom.  I wouldn’t be surprised that ambergris contributes to the mix by joining everything together beautifully.<br />
I find MS to be a serene, peaceful scent that speaks with an Asian tone.  Sillage is moderate, but definitely noticeable, dry down is long-lasting and mesmerizing.  The bottle speaks for itself… <br />
<br />
I hope I never empty my bottle.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="799833"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=799833#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent795131" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1043008">minag</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2017-02-21">02/21/17 14:10</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Mortal Skin is an olfactory journey like no other. The opening feels like entering a slick, black cave filled with bats or snakes. The ink is cold, silky smooth, and addictive. The ink gives way to an almost religious experience with the strongly incense-y middle notes - a comforting, warm incense. And at the end, Mortal Skin turns soft, sweet, and woody.<br />
<br />
Stephane Humbert Lucas has certainly created an interesting experience with Mortal Skin. And while I appreciate and admire this experience, it isn't something that I will crave to recreate on a regular basis, so I will satisfy myself with my sample vial. I'm just glad that my skin was able to bring out the full 3 acts of this "play."<br />
<br />
Perhaps I would appreciate it more on a man than myself. The wood and incense is a bit too masculine for me to wear with confidence. Beautiful and enchanting nonetheless.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="795131"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=795131#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent786103" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/419643">Vlud</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2016-11-02">11/02/16 12:16</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Opens up very inky, leathery with a smoky undertone. It envelops you in a witchy, poisonous aura, it really stands out for its name.<br />
One of the most original perfumes that I've ever tried, very dense, deep and hypnotising.<br />
<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/833680">PurseJunkie</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2016-07-11">07/11/16 02:49</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The opening is wonderful with a leathery, resinous smell overlaid by serious blackberry.  There's a bit of stemmy-greenness, too, as befits a blackberry patch, and a lovely clay-like scent as well.  The blackberry is wonderfully fruity without being childish.  I’ve tried this perfume half a dozen times now, and I find this phase lasts anywhere from 15 to 90 minutes, depending on the day and my luck.  Some days I get unlucky and get almost no blackberry at all, though the resin/clay is always there, if perhaps briefly.  <br />
<br />
After that it devolves into a pleasant, but not terribly interesting floral.  Unfortunately, this is something I’ve found all too common with 777 scents (Black Gemstone, O Hira and especially Qom Chilom): an amazing opening with a questionable follow-through.  If they were selling at drugstore/Demeter prices (or if I were a much wealthier woman) I’d be happy enough to them in bulk and spend all day respraying myself, but at six bucks a milliliter I need them to do better, longer.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/628310">rossyegio5</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2015-10-11">10/11/15 03:06</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Profumo complicato, caleidoscopico, intenzionalmente confuso.<br />
Io sento tante spezie (in primis cardamomo), non variopinte ma ammantate da una scura dolcezza.<br />
Emergono, da un velo d'incenso, piccole dense bolle di more, ciliegie, amarene e castagne sotto spirito. Leggo in piramide olfattiva la presenza di tequila ma io sento il classico liquore italiano utile per conservare le amarene.<br />
Il sottofondo è ambra fruttata, resinoso labdano viola addolcito da mirra.<br />
Il nome è altamente drammatico...<br />
Lo cambierei da Mortal Skin in Mora Skin, data la prevalenza della nota.<br />
Inusuale e costosissimo.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="637817"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=637817#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent634663" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/516615">SumoTigerCat</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2017-03-07">03/07/17 15:27</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>My husband writes calligraphy at times, and he always uses a fountain pen for general writing.  One of the inks that he uses is a brand “Iroshizuku”.  The colors are rich; the ink is smooth.  The bottles are simple and elegantly beautiful.  When I wear Mortal Skin, I think of the darkest colors of this ink.<br />
<br />
A kind member sent me a sample of Mortal Skin quite some time ago.  I was smitten, but the price at that time was something that I’d only spend on a rare Guerlain… maybe.  So, for many months, I kept stalking online sites with a wild hope of finding one I might afford.  As good fortune would have it, another member with whom I’ve traded several times had an almost full, with total presentation bottle for trade.  I hemmed and hawed, and cursed.  She kindly accepted my trade offer of a very HTF bottle.  I sighed a bit, and then danced for joy!<br />
<br />
Mortal Skin is not similar to the other Stéphane Humbert Lucas fragrances that I’ve tried. In my opinion, this is the nicest one.  Unique in its’ stark beauty.  I adore the ink note that underlies the scent throughout its’ wearing.  If there were such a thing as Blackberry Ink, this would be it.  The other notes that talk to me are the myrrh, incense, artemisia (yes, a faint whiff of absinthe), and cardamom.  I wouldn’t be surprised that ambergris contributes to the mix by joining everything together beautifully.<br />
I find MS to be a serene, peaceful scent that speaks with an Asian tone.  Sillage is moderate, but definitely noticeable, dry down is long-lasting and mesmerizing.  The bottle speaks for itself… <br />
<br />
I hope I never empty my bottle.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="799833"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=799833#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1658778" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Mortal Skin does not smell like anything I've tried, so there's no point of reference but I'll try. Opening and middle I get mainly blackberry, ink, and incense. It smells very cold, very complex, and mysterious. Beyond that, musk, orris, and unique suede comes out.<br />
<br />
A friend described this to me as how he would imagine a snakes skin to smell and I agree. It does have a snake/alligator skin vibe. If I had to compare, it reminds me a little bit of Etat Libre D'Orange Rien, little bit of Tom Ford Fabulous, and Jubilation XXV mixed together. Very interesting option for the cold weather. This is art, but also wearable art that smells good! There's something addictive about this one one. Absolutely bottle worthy.. <br />
<br />
Scent 9.5/10<br />
Performance 7/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="1658778"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=1658778#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1206888" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1206888" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="17seyed"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1165604"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1165604.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="17seyed" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1206888ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1206888" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.77); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1165604">17seyed</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-08-02">08/02/20 23:40</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>W̶h̶o̶ What are you?<br />
<br />
If Stephane Humbert Lucas told me that there's a real snake hidden inside Mortal Skin, I would believe him. The fragrance seems to shed skin and present a different side of itself each time I wear it.<br />
<br />
Sometimes it opens with a beautifully dark and cold blackberry that is spiced up by cardamom, and dries down a wonderful buttery iris laying on a bed of myrrh and almond. This variation reminds me a little bit of Bois d'Argent and Rolling in Love.<br />
<br />
And sometimes, it has a venomous and photorealistic opening of ink that is made even more bitter with artemisia, and dries down to a robust concoction of resinous opoponax with an animallic touch of a combination between musk and ambergris. This variation reminds me a little bit of Tobacco Oud.<br />
<br />
A dark shadow of incense looms over the composition regardless of which variation decides to show itself that day.<br />
<br />
Mortal Skin is what I consider to be my favorite type of estoric niche perfumery, where the artist creates a unique and engaging fragrance that will not only intrigue your olfactory senses, but also pleases them. That's what I love about Mortal Skin; is that all artistic merit aside, it smells GOOD. Unlike many other "niche" fragrances that think they are the pinnacle of innovation just because they reek of fecal oud and other novelty notes.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Or even something with good performance. Especially for that pile of money. I glad i just got the decant, not a bottle. Briefly, it's toothless, soft and close to the skin. Yes, it have some ink or berries or maybe even smoke - but in a very shy way. "Mortal skin"? C'mon - it's more like "little-pink-snake-want-to-be-scary-cologne". So disappointing.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31518"comment_id="1218689"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Mortal-Skin-31518.html?ccid=1218689#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1370301" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;                 if (lang == 'HE') $("a.en2inter").attr("href", function () {
            return this.href.replace(/www.fragrantica.com/, "www.fragrantica.co.il").replace(/perfume/, "perfumes") });
            });
</script>


<script  data-cfasync="false">
    // Check that service workers are supported
    if ('serviceWorker' in navigator) {
        // Use the window load event to keep the page load performant
        window.addEventListener('load', () => {
            navigator.serviceWorker.register('/service-worker.js?v=rtgK1d3eddb45a054fd62fdca9a01c72fbac6');
        });
    }
</script>
